### Overview [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#pkg-overview)

Package strings implements simple functions to manipulate UTF-8 encoded strings.

For information about UTF-8 strings in Go, see https://blog.golang.org/strings.

#### func [Clone](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/clone.go;l=21) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Clone)added in go1.18

```
func Clone(s string) string
```

Clone returns a fresh copy of s. It guarantees to make a copy of s into a new allocation, which can be important when retaining only a small substring of a much larger string. Using Clone can help such programs use less memory. Of course, since using Clone makes a copy, overuse of Clone can make programs use more memory. Clone should typically be used only rarely, and only when profiling indicates that it is needed. For strings of length zero the string "" will be returned and no allocation is made.

#### func [Compare](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/compare.go;l=15) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Compare)added in go1.5

```
func Compare(a, b string) int
```

Compare returns an integer comparing two strings lexicographically. The result will be 0 if a == b, -1 if a < b, and +1 if a > b.

Use Compare when you need to perform a three-way comparison (with [slices.SortFunc](https://pkg.go.dev/slices#SortFunc), for example). It is usually clearer and always faster to use the built-in string comparison operators ==, <, >, and so on.

#### func [Contains](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=62) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Contains)

#### func [ContainsAny](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=67) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#ContainsAny)

```

```

ContainsAny reports whether any Unicode code points in chars are within s.

#### func [ContainsFunc](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=77) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#ContainsFunc)added in go1.21.0

```
func ContainsFunc(s string, f func(rune) bool) bool
```

ContainsFunc reports whether any Unicode code points r within s satisfy f(r).

#### func [ContainsRune](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=72) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#ContainsRune)

```
func ContainsRune(s string, r rune) bool
```

ContainsRune reports whether the Unicode code point r is within s.

#### func [Count](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=42) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Count)

```
func Count(s, substr string) int
```

Count counts the number of non-overlapping instances of substr in s. If substr is an empty string, Count returns 1 + the number of Unicode code points in s.

#### func [Cut](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=1285) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Cut)added in go1.18

```
func Cut(s, sep string) (before, after string, found bool)
```

Cut slices s around the first instance of sep, returning the text before and after sep. The found result reports whether sep appears in s. If sep does not appear in s, cut returns s, "", false.

#### func [CutPrefix](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=1293) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#CutPrefix)added in go1.20

```
func CutPrefix(s, prefix string) (after string, found bool)
```

CutPrefix returns s without the provided leading prefix string and reports whether it found the prefix. If s doesn't start with prefix, CutPrefix returns s, false. If prefix is the empty string, CutPrefix returns s, true.

#### func [CutSuffix](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=1301) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#CutSuffix)added in go1.20

```
func CutSuffix(s, suffix string) (before string, found bool)
```

CutSuffix returns s without the provided ending suffix string and reports whether it found the suffix. If s doesn't end with suffix, CutSuffix returns s, false. If suffix is the empty string, CutSuffix returns s, true.

#### func [EqualFold](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=1194) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#EqualFold)

```
func EqualFold(s, t string) bool
```

EqualFold reports whether s and t, interpreted as UTF-8 strings, are equal under simple Unicode case-folding, which is a more general form of case-insensitivity.

#### func [Fields](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=384) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Fields)

```
func Fields(s string) []string
```

Fields splits the string s around each instance of one or more consecutive white space characters, as defined by [unicode.IsSpace](https://pkg.go.dev/unicode#IsSpace), returning a slice of substrings of s or an empty slice if s contains only white space. Every element of the returned slice is non-empty. Unlike [Split](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Split), leading and trailing runs runs of white space characters are discarded.

<details tabindex="-1" id="example-Fields" class="Documentation-exampleDetails js-exampleContainer" style="box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-optical-sizing: inherit; font-size-adjust: inherit; font-kerning: inherit; font-feature-settings: inherit; font-variation-settings: inherit; font-size: 16px; margin: 1rem 0px 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; display: block;"><summary class="Documentation-exampleDetailsHeader" style="box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-optical-sizing: inherit; font-size-adjust: inherit; font-kerning: inherit; font-feature-settings: inherit; font-variation-settings: inherit; font-size: 16px; margin: 0px 0px 2rem; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; color: rgb(0, 125, 156); cursor: pointer; outline: none; text-decoration: none;">Example<span>&nbsp;</span><a href="https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#example-Fields" title="Go to Example" aria-label="Go to Example" style="box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-optical-sizing: inherit; font-size-adjust: inherit; #### func [FieldsFunc](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=441) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#FieldsFunc)

```
func FieldsFunc(s string, f func(rune) bool) []string
```

FieldsFunc splits the string s at each run of Unicode code points c satisfying f(c) and returns an array of slices of s. If all code points in s satisfy f(c) or the string is empty, an empty slice is returned. Every element of the returned slice is non-empty. Unlike [SplitFunc], leading and trailing runs of code points satisfying f(c) are discarded.

FieldsFunc makes no guarantees about the order in which it calls f(c) and assumes that f always returns the same value for a given c.

#### func [FieldsFuncSeq](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/iter.go;l=116) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#FieldsFuncSeq)added in go1.24.0

```
func FieldsFuncSeq(s string, f func(rune) bool) iter.Seq[string]
```

FieldsFuncSeq returns an iterator over substrings of s split around runs of Unicode code points satisfying f(c). The iterator yields the same strings that would be returned by [FieldsFunc](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#FieldsFunc)(s), but without constructing the slice.

#### func [FieldsSeq](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/iter.go;l=83) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#FieldsSeq)added in go1.24.0

```
func FieldsSeq(s string) iter.Seq[string]
```

FieldsSeq returns an iterator over substrings of s split around runs of whitespace characters, as defined by [unicode.IsSpace](https://pkg.go.dev/unicode#IsSpace). The iterator yields the same strings that would be returned by [Fields](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Fields)(s), but without constructing the slice.

#### func [HasPrefix](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=520) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#HasPrefix)

#### func [HasSuffix](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=525) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#HasSuffix)

#### func [Index](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=1277) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Index)

```
func Index(s, substr string) int
```

Index returns the index of the first instance of substr in s, or -1 if substr is not present in s.

#### func [IndexAny](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=201) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#IndexAny)

```
func IndexAny(s, chars string) int
```

IndexAny returns the index of the first instance of any Unicode code point from chars in s, or -1 if no Unicode code point from chars is present in s.

#### func [IndexByte](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=119) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#IndexByte)added in go1.2

```
func IndexByte(s string, c byte) int
```

IndexByte returns the index of the first instance of c in s, or -1 if c is not present in s.

#### func [IndexFunc](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=916) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#IndexFunc)

```
func IndexFunc(s string, f func(rune) bool) int
```

IndexFunc returns the index into s of the first Unicode code point satisfying f(c), or -1 if none do.

#### func [IndexRune](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=127) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#IndexRune)

```
func IndexRune(s string, r rune) int
```

IndexRune returns the index of the first instance of the Unicode code point r, or -1 if rune is not present in s. If r is [utf8.RuneError](https://pkg.go.dev/unicode/utf8#RuneError), it returns the first instance of any invalid UTF-8 byte sequence.

<details tabindex="-1" id="example-IndexRune" class="Documentation-exampleDetails js-exampleContainer" style="box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-size: 16px; margin: 1rem 0px 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; display: block;"><summary class="Documentation-exampleDetailsHeader" style="box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variation-settings: inherit; font-size: 16px; margin: 0px 0px 2rem; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; color: rgb(0, 125, 156); cursor: pointer; outline: none; text-decoration: none;">Example<span>&nbsp;</span><a href="https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#example-IndexRune" title="Go to Example" aria-label="Go to Example" style="box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-optical-sizing: inherit; font-size-adjust: inherit; font-kerning: inherit; font-feature-settings: inherit; font-variation-settings: inherit; font-size: 16px; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; color: rgb(0, 125, 156); text-decoration: none; opacity: 0;">¶</a></summary><div class="Documentation-exampleDetailsBody" style="box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; #### func [Join](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=487) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Join)

```
func Join(elems []string, sep string) string
```

Join concatenates the elements of its first argument to create a single string. The separator string sep is placed between elements in the resulting string.

#### func [LastIndex](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=82) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#LastIndex)

```
func LastIndex(s, substr string) int
```

LastIndex returns the index of the last instance of substr in s, or -1 if substr is not present in s.

#### func [LastIndexAny](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=235) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#LastIndexAny)

```
func LastIndexAny(s, chars string) int
```

LastIndexAny returns the index of the last instance of any Unicode code point from chars in s, or -1 if no Unicode code point from chars is present in s.

#### func [LastIndexByte](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=285) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#LastIndexByte)added in go1.5

```
func LastIndexByte(s string, c byte) int
```

LastIndexByte returns the index of the last instance of c in s, or -1 if c is not present in s.

#### func [LastIndexFunc](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=922) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#LastIndexFunc)

```
func LastIndexFunc(s string, f func(rune) bool) int
```

LastIndexFunc returns the index into s of the last Unicode code point satisfying f(c), or -1 if none do.

#### func [Lines](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/iter.go;l=18) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Lines)added in go1.24.0

```
func Lines(s string) iter.Seq[string]
```

Lines returns an iterator over the newline-terminated lines in the string s. The lines yielded by the iterator include their terminating newlines. If s is empty, the iterator yields no lines at all. If s does not end in a newline, the final yielded line will not end in a newline. It returns a single-use iterator.

#### func [Map](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=532) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Map)

```
func Map(mapping func(rune) rune, s string) string
```

Map returns a copy of the string s with all its characters modified according to the mapping function. If mapping returns a negative value, the character is dropped from the string with no replacement.

#### func [Repeat](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=616) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Repeat)

```
func Repeat(s string, count int) string
```

Repeat returns a new string consisting of count copies of the string s.

It panics if count is negative or if the result of (len(s) * count) overflows.

#### func [Replace](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=1145) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Replace)

```
func Replace(s, old, new string, n int) string
```

Replace returns a copy of the string s with the first n non-overlapping instances of old replaced by new. If old is empty, it matches at the beginning of the string and after each UTF-8 sequence, yielding up to k+1 replacements for a k-rune string. If n < 0, there is no limit on the number of replacements.

#### func [ReplaceAll](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=1187) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#ReplaceAll)added in go1.12

```
func ReplaceAll(s, old, new string) string
```

ReplaceAll returns a copy of the string s with all non-overlapping instances of old replaced by new. If old is empty, it matches at the beginning of the string and after each UTF-8 sequence, yielding up to k+1 replacements for a k-rune string.

#### func [Split](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=361) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Split)

```
func Split(s, sep string) []string
```

Split slices s into all substrings separated by sep and returns a slice of the substrings between those separators.

If s does not contain sep and sep is not empty, Split returns a slice of length 1 whose only element is s.

If sep is empty, Split splits after each UTF-8 sequence. If both s and sep are empty, Split returns an empty slice.

It is equivalent to [SplitN](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#SplitN) with a count of -1.

To split around the first instance of a separator, see [Cut](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Cut).

#### func [SplitAfter](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=373) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#SplitAfter)

```
func SplitAfter(s, sep string) []string
```

SplitAfter slices s into all substrings after each instance of sep and returns a slice of those substrings.

If s does not contain sep and sep is not empty, SplitAfter returns a slice of length 1 whose only element is s.

If sep is empty, SplitAfter splits after each UTF-8 sequence. If both s and sep are empty, SplitAfter returns an empty slice.

It is equivalent to [SplitAfterN](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#SplitAfterN) with a count of -1.

#### func [SplitAfterN](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=345) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#SplitAfterN)

```
func SplitAfterN(s, sep string, n int) []string
```

SplitAfterN slices s into substrings after each instance of sep and returns a slice of those substrings.

The count determines the number of substrings to return:

- n > 0: at most n substrings; the last substring will be the unsplit remainder;
- n == 0: the result is nil (zero substrings);
- n < 0: all substrings.

Edge cases for s and sep (for example, empty strings) are handled as described in the documentation for [SplitAfter](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#SplitAfter).

#### func [SplitAfterSeq](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/iter.go;l=75) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#SplitAfterSeq)added in go1.24.0

```
func SplitAfterSeq(s, sep string) iter.Seq[string]
```

SplitAfterSeq returns an iterator over substrings of s split after each instance of sep. The iterator yields the same strings that would be returned by [SplitAfter](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#SplitAfter)(s, sep), but without constructing the slice. It returns a single-use iterator.

#### func [SplitN](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=333) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#SplitN)

```
func SplitN(s, sep string, n int) []string
```

SplitN slices s into substrings separated by sep and returns a slice of the substrings between those separators.

The count determines the number of substrings to return:

- n > 0: at most n substrings; the last substring will be the unsplit remainder;
- n == 0: the result is nil (zero substrings);
- n < 0: all substrings.

Edge cases for s and sep (for example, empty strings) are handled as described in the documentation for [Split](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Split).

To split around the first instance of a separator, see [Cut](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Cut).

#### func [SplitSeq](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/iter.go;l=67) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#SplitSeq)added in go1.24.0

```
func SplitSeq(s, sep string) iter.Seq[string]
```

SplitSeq returns an iterator over all substrings of s separated by sep. The iterator yields the same strings that would be returned by [Split](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Split)(s, sep), but without constructing the slice. It returns a single-use iterator.

#### func [ToLower](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=727) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#ToLower)

```
func ToLower(s string) string
```

ToLower returns s with all Unicode letters mapped to their lower case.

#### func [ToLowerSpecial](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=778) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#ToLowerSpecial)

```
func ToLowerSpecial(c unicode.SpecialCase, s string) string
```

ToLowerSpecial returns a copy of the string s with all Unicode letters mapped to their lower case using the case mapping specified by c.

<details tabindex="-1" id="example-ToLowerSpecial" class="Documentation-exampleDetails js-exampleContainer" style="box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-optical-sizing: inherit; font-size-adjust: inherit; font-kerning: inherit; font-feature-settings: inherit; font-variation-settings: inherit; font-size: 16px; margin: 1rem 0px 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; display: block;"><summary class="Documentation-exampleDetailsHeader" style="box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-optical-sizing: inherit; font-size-adjust: inherit; font-kerning: inherit; font-feature-settings: inherit; font-variation-settings: inherit; font-size: 16px; margin: 0px 0px 2rem; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; color: rgb(0, 125, 156); cursor: pointer; outline: none; text-decoration: none;">Example<span>&nbsp;</span><a href="https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#example-ToLowerSpecial" title="Go to Example" aria-label="Go to Example" style="box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; font-stretch: inherit; line-height: inherit; font-family: inherit; font-optical-sizing: inherit; font-size-adjust: inherit; font-kerning: inherit; font-feature-settings: inherit; font-variation-settings: inherit; font-size: 16px; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; vertical-align: baseline; color: rgb(0, 125, 156); text-decoration: none; #### func [ToTitle](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=768) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#ToTitle)

```

```

ToTitle returns a copy of the string s with all Unicode letters mapped to their Unicode title case.

#### func [ToTitleSpecial](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=784) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#ToTitleSpecial)

```
func ToTitleSpecial(c unicode.SpecialCase, s string) string
```

ToTitleSpecial returns a copy of the string s with all Unicode letters mapped to their Unicode title case, giving priority to the special casing rules.

#### func [ToUpper](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=687) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#ToUpper)

```

```

#### func [ToUpperSpecial](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=772) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#ToUpperSpecial)

```
func ToUpperSpecial(c unicode.SpecialCase, s string) string
```

ToUpperSpecial returns a copy of the string s with all Unicode letters mapped to their upper case using the case mapping specified by c.

#### func [ToValidUTF8](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=790) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#ToValidUTF8)added in go1.13

```
func ToValidUTF8(s, replacement string) string
```

ToValidUTF8 returns a copy of the string s with each run of invalid UTF-8 byte sequences replaced by the replacement string, which may be empty.

#### func [Trim](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=982) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Trim)

```
func Trim(s, cutset string) string
```

Trim returns a slice of the string s with all leading and trailing Unicode code points contained in cutset removed.

#### func [TrimFunc](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=910) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#TrimFunc)

```
func TrimFunc(s string, f func(rune) bool) string
```

TrimFunc returns a slice of the string s with all leading and trailing Unicode code points c satisfying f(c) removed.

#### func [TrimLeft](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=999) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#TrimLeft)

```
func TrimLeft(s, cutset string) string
```

TrimLeft returns a slice of the string s with all leading Unicode code points contained in cutset removed.

To remove a prefix, use [TrimPrefix](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#TrimPrefix) instead.

#### func [TrimLeftFunc](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=887) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#TrimLeftFunc)

```
func TrimLeftFunc(s string, f func(rune) bool) string
```

TrimLeftFunc returns a slice of the string s with all leading Unicode code points c satisfying f(c) removed.

#### func [TrimPrefix](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=1129) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#TrimPrefix)added in go1.1

```
func TrimPrefix(s, prefix string) string
```

TrimPrefix returns s without the provided leading prefix string. If s doesn't start with prefix, s is returned unchanged.

#### func [TrimRight](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=1047) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#TrimRight)

```
func TrimRight(s, cutset string) string
```

TrimRight returns a slice of the string s, with all trailing Unicode code points contained in cutset removed.

To remove a suffix, use [TrimSuffix](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#TrimSuffix) instead.

#### func [TrimRightFunc](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=897) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#TrimRightFunc)

```
func TrimRightFunc(s string, f func(rune) bool) string
```

TrimRightFunc returns a slice of the string s with all trailing Unicode code points c satisfying f(c) removed.

#### func [TrimSpace](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=1093) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#TrimSpace)

```
func TrimSpace(s string) string
```

TrimSpace returns a slice of the string s, with all leading and trailing white space removed, as defined by Unicode.

#### func [TrimSuffix](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/strings.go;l=1135) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#TrimSuffix)added in go1.1

```
func TrimSuffix(s, suffix string) string
```

TrimSuffix returns s without the provided trailing suffix string. If s doesn't end with suffix, s is returned unchanged.

### Types [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#pkg-types)

#### type [Builder](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/builder.go;l=17) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Builder)added in go1.10

```
type Builder struct {
	// contains filtered or unexported fields
}
```

A Builder is used to efficiently build a string using [Builder.Write](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Builder.Write) methods. It minimizes memory copying. The zero value is ready to use. Do not copy a non-zero Builder.

<details tabindex="-1" id="example-Builder" class="Documentation-exampleDetails js-exampleContainer" style="box-sizing: border-box; border: 0px; font-style: inherit; font-variant: inherit; font-weight: inherit; #### func (*Builder) [Cap](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/builder.go;l=56) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Builder.Cap)added in go1.12

```
func (b *Builder) Cap() int
```

Cap returns the capacity of the builder's underlying byte slice. It is the total space allocated for the string being built and includes any bytes already written.

#### func (*Builder) [Grow](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/builder.go;l=75) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Builder.Grow)added in go1.10

```
func (b *Builder) Grow(n int)
```

Grow grows b's capacity, if necessary, to guarantee space for another n bytes. After Grow(n), at least n bytes can be written to b without another allocation. If n is negative, Grow panics.

#### func (*Builder) [Len](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/builder.go;l=51) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Builder.Len)added in go1.10

```
func (b *Builder) Len() int
```

Len returns the number of accumulated bytes; b.Len() == len(b.String()).

#### func (*Builder) [Reset](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/builder.go;l=59) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Builder.Reset)added in go1.10

```
func (b *Builder) Reset()
```

Reset resets the [Builder](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Builder) to be empty.

#### func (*Builder) [String](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/builder.go;l=46) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Builder.String)added in go1.10

```
func (b *Builder) String() string
```

String returns the accumulated string.

#### func (*Builder) [Write](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/builder.go;l=87) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Builder.Write)added in go1.10

```
func (b *Builder) Write(p []byte) (int, error)
```

Write appends the contents of p to b's buffer. Write always returns len(p), nil.

#### func (*Builder) [WriteByte](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/builder.go;l=95) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Builder.WriteByte)added in go1.10

```
func (b *Builder) WriteByte(c byte) error
```

WriteByte appends the byte c to b's buffer. The returned error is always nil.

#### func (*Builder) [WriteRune](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/builder.go;l=103) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Builder.WriteRune)added in go1.10

```
func (b *Builder) WriteRune(r rune) (int, error)
```

WriteRune appends the UTF-8 encoding of Unicode code point r to b's buffer. It returns the length of r and a nil error.

#### func (*Builder) [WriteString](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/builder.go;l=112) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Builder.WriteString)added in go1.10

```
func (b *Builder) WriteString(s string) (int, error)
```

WriteString appends the contents of s to b's buffer. It returns the length of s and a nil error.

#### type [Reader](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/reader.go;l=17) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Reader)

```
type Reader struct {
	// contains filtered or unexported fields
}
```

A Reader implements the [io.Reader](https://pkg.go.dev/io#Reader), [io.ReaderAt](https://pkg.go.dev/io#ReaderAt), [io.ByteReader](https://pkg.go.dev/io#ByteReader), [io.ByteScanner](https://pkg.go.dev/io#ByteScanner), [io.RuneReader](https://pkg.go.dev/io#RuneReader), [io.RuneScanner](https://pkg.go.dev/io#RuneScanner), [io.Seeker](https://pkg.go.dev/io#Seeker), and [io.WriterTo](https://pkg.go.dev/io#WriterTo) interfaces by reading from a string. The zero value for Reader operates like a Reader of an empty string.

#### func [NewReader](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/reader.go;l=160) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#NewReader)

```
func NewReader(s string) *Reader
```

NewReader returns a new [Reader](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Reader) reading from s. It is similar to [bytes.NewBufferString](https://pkg.go.dev/bytes#NewBufferString) but more efficient and non-writable.

#### func (*Reader) [Len](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/reader.go;l=25) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Reader.Len)

```
func (r *Reader) Len() int
```

Len returns the number of bytes of the unread portion of the string.

#### func (*Reader) [Read](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/reader.go;l=39) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Reader.Read)

```
func (r *Reader) Read(b []byte) (n int, err error)
```

Read implements the [io.Reader](https://pkg.go.dev/io#Reader) interface.

#### func (*Reader) [ReadAt](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/reader.go;l=50) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Reader.ReadAt)

```
func (r *Reader) ReadAt(b []byte, off int64) (n int, err error)
```

ReadAt implements the [io.ReaderAt](https://pkg.go.dev/io#ReaderAt) interface.

#### func (*Reader) [ReadByte](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/reader.go;l=66) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Reader.ReadByte)

```
func (r *Reader) ReadByte() (byte, error)
```

ReadByte implements the [io.ByteReader](https://pkg.go.dev/io#ByteReader) interface.

#### func (*Reader) [ReadRune](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/reader.go;l=87) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Reader.ReadRune)

```
func (r *Reader) ReadRune() (ch rune, size int, err error)
```

ReadRune implements the [io.RuneReader](https://pkg.go.dev/io#RuneReader) interface.

#### func (*Reader) [Reset](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/reader.go;l=156) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Reader.Reset)added in go1.7

```
func (r *Reader) Reset(s string)
```

Reset resets the [Reader](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Reader) to be reading from s.

#### func (*Reader) [Seek](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/reader.go;l=116) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Reader.Seek)

```
func (r *Reader) Seek(offset int64, whence int) (int64, error)
```

Seek implements the [io.Seeker](https://pkg.go.dev/io#Seeker) interface.

#### func (*Reader) [Size](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/reader.go;l=36) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Reader.Size)added in go1.5

```
func (r *Reader) Size() int64
```

Size returns the original length of the underlying string. Size is the number of bytes available for reading via [Reader.ReadAt](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Reader.ReadAt). The returned value is always the same and is not affected by calls to any other method.

#### func (*Reader) [UnreadByte](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/reader.go;l=77) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Reader.UnreadByte)

```
func (r *Reader) UnreadByte() error
```

UnreadByte implements the [io.ByteScanner](https://pkg.go.dev/io#ByteScanner) interface.

#### func (*Reader) [UnreadRune](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/reader.go;l=103) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Reader.UnreadRune)

```
func (r *Reader) UnreadRune() error
```

UnreadRune implements the [io.RuneScanner](https://pkg.go.dev/io#RuneScanner) interface.

#### func (*Reader) [WriteTo](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/reader.go;l=137) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Reader.WriteTo)added in go1.1

```
func (r *Reader) WriteTo(w io.Writer) (n int64, err error)
```

WriteTo implements the [io.WriterTo](https://pkg.go.dev/io#WriterTo) interface.

#### type [Replacer](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/replace.go;l=14) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Replacer)

```
type Replacer struct {
	// contains filtered or unexported fields
}
```

Replacer replaces a list of strings with replacements. It is safe for concurrent use by multiple goroutines.

#### func [NewReplacer](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/replace.go;l=32) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#NewReplacer)

```
func NewReplacer(oldnew ...string) *Replacer
```

NewReplacer returns a new [Replacer](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Replacer) from a list of old, new string pairs. Replacements are performed in the order they appear in the target string, without overlapping matches. The old string comparisons are done in argument order.

NewReplacer panics if given an odd number of arguments.

#### func (*Replacer) [Replace](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/replace.go;l=95) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Replacer.Replace)

```
func (r *Replacer) Replace(s string) string
```

Replace returns a copy of s with all replacements performed.

#### func (*Replacer) [WriteString](https://cs.opensource.google/go/go/+/go1.25.0:src/strings/replace.go;l=101) [¶](https://pkg.go.dev/strings@go1.25.0#Replacer.WriteString)

```
func (r *Replacer) WriteString(w io.Writer, s string) (n int, err error)
```

WriteString writes s to w with all replacements performed.
